# API Evangelist Network

A network index of all APIs.json files maintained by the API Evangelist organization, providing a comprehensive directory of API definitions across the network.

- **Total repos:** 10209
- **Last updated:** 2026-07-02
- **Specification version:** 0.19

Providers only — API Evangelist infrastructure repositories and topical
repositories are intentionally excluded; [apievangelist.com](https://apievangelist.com)
is the front door for those.
